</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span></code></pre></div></div><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">2. Control Flow in Rust</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Rust, as the initial implementation language, manages control flow by:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Defining the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">control_flow</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> field as a vector of Pubkeys, representing possible next blocks (e.g., sequential execution, conditional branches, or loops).</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Using a Solana program to traverse the control flow graph during execution.</span></span></span></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Control Flow Logic</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Sequential Execution</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: A block points to a single successor (e.g., </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">block0 -&gt; block1</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">).</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Branches</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: A block points to multiple successors based on conditions (e.g., </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">if r1 == 0 then block2 else block3</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">).</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Loops/Calls</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Blocks reference other functions or themselves for loops.</span></span></span></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Example Solana program snippet for executing a basic block:</span></span></span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-1adg3ll r-ag158w r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi r-13qz1uu"><div class="css-175oi2r r-dnmrzs r-1adg3ll r-13qz1uu" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-1fkb3t2 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">rust</span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5 r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.3; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; padding: 12px; margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; overflow: auto; background: rgb(22, 24, 28); display: block; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom-left-radius: 8px; border-bottom-right-radius: 8px;"><code class="language-rust" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">fn</span><span> </span><span class="token function-definition" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">execute_block</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>
</span><span>    accounts</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&amp;</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">AccountInfo</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    block_acc</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&amp;</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">AccountInfo</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">-&gt;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">ProgramResult</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">let</span><span> block_data </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">BasicBlockAccount</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">::</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">try_from_slice</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&amp;</span><span>block_acc</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>data</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">borrow</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">?</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Fetch instructions from side chain using storage_hash</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">let</span><span> instructions </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">fetch_from_side_chain</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>block_data</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>storage_hash</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">?</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Execute instructions (e.g., via WASM runtime)</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">execute_instructions</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>instructions</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">?</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Get next block from control_flow</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">let</span><span> next_block </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> block_data</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>control_flow</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">get</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">ok_or</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">ProgramError</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">::</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">InvalidInstructionData</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">?</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Trigger execution of next block</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">Ok</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span></code></pre></div></div><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Control Flow Example</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:
For a function </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">connect(a, b)</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">block0</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Load inputs (</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">mov r1, a</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">).</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">block1</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Branch (</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">if r1 == 0 then block3 else block2</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">).</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">block2</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Call </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">transfer</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> function.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">block3</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Return.
The </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">BasicBlockAccount</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> for </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">block1</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> has </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">control_flow: [block2_pubkey, block3_pubkey]</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.</span></span></span></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">3. Transition to Lean4</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Lean4, a dependently typed language and theorem prover, is introduced later to formalize control flow, leveraging univalent principles and the RDF ontology. Lean4’s strengths include:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Dependent Types</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Ensure that control flow transitions respect type constraints (e.g., a block’s output type matches the next block’s input type).</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Formal Verification</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Prove correctness of control flow graphs, ensuring no invalid transitions or unreachable blocks.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Univalent Foundations</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Encode equivalences and identity types for blocks and functions, aligning with the system’s univalent inspiration.</span></span></span></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Lean4 Integration</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Control Flow Specification</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Define the control flow graph in Lean4, using dependent types to model transitions. Example:</span></span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-1adg3ll r-ag158w r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi r-13qz1uu"><div class="css-175oi2r r-dnmrzs r-1adg3ll r-13qz1uu" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-1fkb3t2 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">lean</span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5 r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.3; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; padding: 12px; margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; overflow: auto; background: rgb(22, 24, 28); display: block; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom-left-radius: 8px; border-bottom-right-radius: 8px;"><code class="language-text" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span>inductive BlockID : Type
</span>| mk : String → BlockID

inductive ControlFlow : BlockID → BlockID → Type
| sequential : ∀ (b1 b2 : BlockID), ControlFlow b1 b2
| branch : ∀ (b1 b2 b3 : BlockID), Bool → ControlFlow b1 (if b then b2 else b3)

def valid_transition (b1 b2 : BlockID) : Prop :=
  ∃ cf : ControlFlow b1 b2, True</code></pre></div></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Side Chain Storage</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Store Lean4 specifications (e.g., control flow proofs) on the side chain, referenced by </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">storage_hash</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">. Example:</span></span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-1adg3ll r-ag158w r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi r-13qz1uu"><div class="css-175oi2r r-dnmrzs r-1adg3ll r-13qz1uu" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-1fkb3t2 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">json</span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5 r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.3; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; padding: 12px; margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; overflow: auto; background: rgb(22, 24, 28); display: block; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom-left-radius: 8px; border-bottom-right-radius: 8px;"><code class="language-json" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>

</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span></code></pre></div></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Verification</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: During execution, the Solana program invokes a Lean4 verifier (e.g., via a side chain WASM runtime) to check that block transitions satisfy the Lean4 specification.</span></span></span></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Transition Plan</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Phase 1 (Rust)</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Implement control flow using Rust structs and Solana transactions. The </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">control_flow</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> field is a simple Pubkey vector, and execution is straightforward but not formally verified.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Phase 2 (Lean4)</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Replace Rust-based control flow logic with Lean4 specifications. Each </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">BasicBlockAccount</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> includes a </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">storage_hash</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> linking to a Lean4 proof of valid transitions. The side chain runs a Lean4 verifier to ensure correctness before execution.</span></span></span></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">4. RDF Ontology Integration</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The RDF-like ontology ties basic blocks, functions, and types together:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Triples</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">(Function_connect, hasBlock, Block0)</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Links a function to its blocks.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">(Block0, hasNext, Block1)</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Encodes control flow as an RDF relationship.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">(Block0, rdf:type, FunctionType)</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Ties blocks to the type system.</span></span></span></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Side Chain</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Stores the full ontology graph, with Solana accounts holding hashes. Side Chain and Transparent Storage</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The side chain, with no storage or compute limits, handles:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Instructions</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Full bytecode for basic blocks, beyond what fits in Solana accounts.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; ### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1x3r274 r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">we will use llvm, so the llvm ir will be ported, lean4 and rust iteself will live on this side chain. maybe we have a dedicated chain for each project.</span></span></span></span>

### Grok AI

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 (Intermediate Representation) for basic blocks, storing </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> and </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-poiln3"> code on the side chain, and potentially dedicating a </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">separate side chain for each project</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">. This builds on the existing framework where types, functions, and basic blocks are Solana accounts (spaces), control flow is managed via a </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">control_flow</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> field (initially in Rust, later Lean4), and a side chain with transparent backend storage eliminates limits. The use of LLVM IR provides a standardized, portable representation for basic blocks, while per-project side chains enhance modularity and scalability. Let’s refine the design, focusing on these additions, while keeping it concise and consistent with prior details.</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Updated System Design</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">1. LLVM IR for Basic Blocks</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Using </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">LLVM</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">, each binary is compiled into </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">LLVM IR</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">, which is then split into functions and basic blocks, with each basic block stored as a Solana account. LLVM IR is a portable, low-level intermediate representation, ideal for modular execution and optimization.</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; </span><span>    block_id</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">String</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>         </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// e.g., "func1_block0"</span><span>
</span><span>    function_id</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">String</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>      </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Parent function (e.g., "connect")</span><span>
</span><span>    llvm_ir</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">Vec</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&lt;</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">u8</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>         </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Serialized LLVM IR for the block</span><span>
</span><span>    control_flow</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">Vec</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&lt;</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">Pubkey</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Successor blocks</span><span>
</span><span>    type_id</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">Pubkey</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>          </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Associated type (e.g., "FunctionType")</span><span>
</span><span>    storage_hash</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">u8</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">32</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>   </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Side chain hash for full IR or metadata</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span></code></pre></div></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Porting LLVM IR</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">LLVM IR is platform-agnostic, allowing basic blocks to be executed on a side chain runtime (e.g., WASM or a custom LLVM interpreter).</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">llvm_ir</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> field stores a compact subset of instructions, with the full IR or additional metadata on the side chain, referenced via </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">storage_hash</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.</span></span></span></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Execution</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">A Solana transaction triggers execution of a basic block by fetching its LLVM IR (from the account or side chain).</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">A side chain runtime (e.g., LLVM JIT or WASM) executes the IR, following the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">control_flow</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> links.</span></span></span></li></ul></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">2. Lean4 and Rust on the Side Chain</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">You specify that </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Lean4</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> (for formal control flow verification) and </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Rust</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> (for system implementation) live on the side chain, meaning their source code, compilers, and runtime environments are stored and executed there.</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Storage</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Rust</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Source code, </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">rustc</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> compiler, and compiled binaries (e.g., Solana programs) are stored on the side chain, referenced by hashes in Solana accounts.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Lean4</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Source specifications, Lean4 prover, and compiled artifacts (e.g., WASM or native binaries) are stored similarly.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Example side chain entry:</span></span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-1adg3ll r-ag158w r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi r-13qz1uu"><div class="css-175oi2r r-dnmrzs r-1adg3ll r-13qz1uu" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-1fkb3t2 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">json</span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5 r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Rust code (e.g., Solana programs) is compiled on the side chain and deployed to Solana.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Lean4 verifies control flow graphs during block execution, running on a side chain WASM runtime.</span></span></span></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Lisp-Like ASTs</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Both Rust and Lean4 code are represented as ASTs (e.g., S-expressions or RDF triples) for dynamic manipulation, aligning with the Lisp-inspired philosophy.</span></span></span></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">3. Dedicated Side Chain per Project</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">You propose a </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">dedicated side chain for each project</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">, enhancing modularity, isolation, and scalability. Each project (e.g., a DApp, smart contract, or ontology) has its own side chain, storing its types, functions, basic blocks, and artifacts (Rust, Lean4, LLVM IR).</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Side Chain Structure</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">A project-specific side chain (e.g., a Solana layer-2 or custom blockchain) with:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Storage</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: IPFS, Arweave, or a database for LLVM IR, ASTs, Rust/Lean4 code.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Runtime</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: WASM or LLVM JIT for executing basic blocks and Lean4 verifications.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Validator</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Ensures data integrity and syncs with the Solana main chain.</span></span></span></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Solana accounts store </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">storage_hash</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> linking to the project’s side chain.</span></span></span></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Interoperability</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Projects interact via Solana transactions, with cross-chain references (e.g., a </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">TypeAccount</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> in Project A references a </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">BasicBlockAccount</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> in Project B).</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The Solana main chain anchors trust, while side chains handle project-specific logic.</span></span></span></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Benefits</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Isolation</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Each project’s ontology, code, and execution environment is self-contained.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Scalability</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: No contention for side chain resources across projects.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Customization</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">: Project-specific optimizations (e.g., tailored Lean4 proofs).</span></span></span></li></ul></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">4. Control Flow (Rust → Lean4)</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Control flow between basic blocks is managed via the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">control_flow</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> field, initially in Rust, with a transition to Lean4 for formal verification.</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Rust Implementation</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">control_flow</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> field lists successor Pubkeys, enabling sequential, branching, or looping execution.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Example: For </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">block0</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> (load) → </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">block1</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> (branch), </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">block0</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">’s </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">control_flow: [block1_pubkey]</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; padding: 12px; margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; overflow: auto; background: rgb(22, 24, 28); display: block; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom-left-radius: 8px; border-bottom-right-radius: 8px;"><code class="language-text" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span>inductive BlockID : Type
</span>| mk : String → BlockID

def ControlFlow : BlockID → BlockID → Type
| sequential : ∀ b1 b2, ControlFlow b1 b2
| branch : ∀ b1 b2 b3, Bool → ControlFlow b1 (if b then b2 else b3)

def valid_path (b1 b2 : BlockID) : Prop := ∃ cf : ControlFlow b1 b2, True</code></pre></div></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Side chain stores Lean4 proofs, verified before block execution:</span></span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-1adg3ll r-ag158w r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi r-13qz1uu"><div class="css-175oi2r r-dnmrzs r-1adg3ll r-13qz1uu" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-1fkb3t2 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">rust</span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5 r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); RDF Ontology Integration</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The RDF-like ontology links types, functions, and basic blocks:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Triples</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; </span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span></code></pre></div></div><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">7. ### User

<span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1x3r274 r-p1pxzi"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">LVM Integration: Parsing and executing LLVM IR on the side chain requires a robust runtime. that runtime is solana that we will compile llvm to live in.</span></span></span></span>
