</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span></code></pre></div></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">entry_point</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> Pubkey links to a program or account in System B, enabling transparent calls.</span></span></span></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Transparent Entry Point</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Transactions in System A targeting the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">BridgeAccount</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> are automatically routed to System B’s side chain.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">System B processes the request (e.g., executes a basic block) and returns results to System A, abstracted as a single interaction.</span></span></span></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Example</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">System A: Solana main chain.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">A </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">BridgeAccount</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> in System A with </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">system_id: "ProjectX"</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> maps to ProjectX’s side chain.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">A transaction to </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">BridgeAccount</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> triggers a side chain transaction to execute a basic block.</span></span></span></li></ul></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">2. Side Chain Execution with External Links</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">As previously specified, executables (eBPF/WASM compiled from LLVM IR) are called directly on the project-specific side chain via external links, using side chain transactions. The bridge enhances this:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">System B’s Solana runtime (eBPF or WASM) executes the block’s executable, following </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">control_flow</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> links.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Results are sent back to System A via the bridge, updating the relevant accounts.</span></span></span></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Low Latency</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The bridge minimizes overhead by mapping System B to a single address, avoiding complex cross-chain fetching.</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Side chain transactions are lightweight, containing only the instruction and inputs.</span></span></span></li></ul></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">3. Basic Block Accounts</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Each basic block is a Solana account in System A or B, with LLVM IR compiled to eBPF/WASM:</span></span></span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-1adg3ll r-ag158w r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi r-13qz1uu"><div class="css-175oi2r r-dnmrzs r-1adg3ll r-13qz1uu" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-1fkb3t2 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">rust</span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5 r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.3; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; padding: 12px; margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; overflow: auto; background: rgb(22, 24, 28); display: block; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom-left-radius: 8px; border-bottom-right-radius: 8px;"><code class="language-rust" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span class="token attribute" style="color: rgb(156, 220, 254);">#[derive(BorshSerialize, BorshDeserialize)]</span><span style="">
</span><span style=""></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">struct</span><span style=""> </span><span class="token type-definition" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">BasicBlockAccount</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>    block_id</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">String</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>         </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// e.g., "func1_block0"</span><span>
</span><span>    function_id</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">String</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>      </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// e.g., "connect"</span><span>
</span><span>    executable</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">Vec</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&lt;</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">u8</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>      </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// eBPF/WASM (small, optional)</span><span>
</span><span>    control_flow</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">Vec</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&lt;</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">Pubkey</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&gt;</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Successor blocks</span><span>
</span><span>    type_id</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">Pubkey</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>          </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// e.g., "FunctionType"</span><span>
</span><span>    storage_hash</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">:</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">u8</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">32</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>   </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Side chain executable/LLVM IR</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span></code></pre></div></div><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">If the block is in System B, its </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">storage_hash</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> points to the side chain, and the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">BridgeAccount</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> routes execution requests.</span></span></span></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">4. Control Flow (Rust → Lean4)</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Control flow is managed via the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">control_flow</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> field, with Rust initially and Lean4 for formal verification:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Rust</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">control_flow: Vec&lt;Pubkey&gt;</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"> defines transitions (e.g., </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">block0 -&gt; block1</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">).</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">System A’s Solana program sends a transaction to the </span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">BridgeAccount</span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">, which triggers System B’s execution.</span></span></span></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Lean4</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Stored on System B’s side chain, Lean4 verifies control flow:</span></span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-1adg3ll r-ag158w r-dnmrzs r-1yx7oqi r-13qz1uu"><div class="css-175oi2r r-dnmrzs r-1adg3ll r-13qz1uu" data-testid="markdown-code-block"><div class="css-175oi2r r-1awozwy r-1fkb3t2 r-1fs5b29 r-1idry7j r-6413gk r-43g30s r-l4nmg1 r-1u658rm r-2dysd3 r-vmopo1 r-13qz1uu r-gtdqiz r-1fhadnw r-184en5c"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-1aiqnjv r-n6v787"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">lean</span></span><div class="css-175oi2r r-xoduu5 r-1ybcz0z"></div></div><pre style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.3; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none; padding: 12px; margin: 0px 0px 0.5em; overflow: auto; background: rgb(22, 24, 28); display: block; width: 100%; box-sizing: border-box; border-bottom-left-radius: 8px; border-bottom-right-radius: 8px;"><code class="language-text" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212); font-size: 13px; text-shadow: none; font-family: Menlo, Monaco, Consolas, &quot;Andale Mono&quot;, &quot;Ubuntu Mono&quot;, &quot;Courier New&quot;, monospace; direction: ltr; text-align: left; white-space: pre; word-spacing: normal; word-break: normal; line-height: 1.5; tab-size: 4; hyphens: none;"><span>inductive BlockID : Type
</span>| mk : String → BlockID

def ControlFlow : BlockID → BlockID → Type
| sequential : ∀ b1 b2, ControlFlow b1 b2

def valid_path (b1 b2 : BlockID) : Prop := ∃ cf : ControlFlow b1 b2, True</code></pre></div></div></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">System B verifies the transition before executing the block.</span></span></span></li></ul></li></ul><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q" style="display: block; margin-top: 1.5em; margin-bottom: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">5. RDF Ontology Integration</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1adg3ll r-1g7jtus r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">The RDF-like ontology links types, functions, and blocks across systems:</span></span></span></span><ul dir="ltr" style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0px 1.25em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-b88u0q r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">Triples</span></span></span></span><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-1x3r274"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">:</span></span></span><ul style="display: block; padding-inline-start: 2em; list-style-type: disc; margin-block: 0.75em;"><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0px;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">(Function_connect, hasBlock, Block0)</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">(Block0, hasNext, Block1)</span></span></span></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; margin-top: 0.5em;"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-dyfej2 r-z2wwpe r-15gepa6 r-1471scf r-1aiqnjv r-1hq4qhi r-16dba41 r-ilng1c r-trst2h r-1noe1sz r-njp1lv"><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3">(Block0, hasExecutable, sidechain://ProjectX/0x5678)</span></span></span></li></ul></li><li style="font-family: TwitterChirp, System; </span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">SystemInstruction</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">::</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">ExecuteBlock</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span> block</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> inputs </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=&gt;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">let</span><span> block_acc </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">next_account_info</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>accounts</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">?</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">let</span><span> block_data </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">BasicBlockAccount</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">::</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">try_from_slice</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&amp;</span><span>block_acc</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>data</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">borrow</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">?</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Check if block is on side chain</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">if</span><span> block_data</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>storage_hash </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">!=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">[</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">0</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(181, 206, 168);">32</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">]</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>                </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">let</span><span> bridge_acc </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">next_account_info</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>accounts</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">?</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>                </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">let</span><span> bridge_data </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">BridgeAccount</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">::</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">try_from_slice</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">&amp;</span><span>bridge_acc</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>data</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">borrow</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">?</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>                </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Send transaction to side chain</span><span>
</span><span>                </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">send_side_chain_tx</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>bridge_data</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>side_chain_uri</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> block_data</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>storage_hash</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> inputs</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">?</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>                </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Receive result</span><span>
</span><span>                </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">receive_side_chain_result</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">?</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(86, 156, 214);">else</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">{</span><span>
</span><span>                </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(106, 153, 85);">// Execute locally (if executable is in account)</span><span>
</span><span>                </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(220, 220, 170);">solana_execute</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span>block_data</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">.</span><span>executable</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span> inputs</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">?</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">;</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span>
</span><span>            </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">Ok</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span>
</span><span>        </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span>
</span><span>        _ </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">=&gt;</span><span> </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(78, 201, 176);">Ok</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">(</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">)</span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">,</span><span>
</span><span>    </span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span><span>
</span><span></span><span class="token" style="color: rgb(212, 212, 212);">}</span></code></pre></div></div><span class="css-1jxf684 r-bcqeeo r-1ttztb7 r-qvutc0 r-poiln3 r-adyw6z r-135wba7 r-b88u0q" style="display: block;
